       $(document).ready(function(){
                                $(".fancy-input").keyup(function(){
                                    if ($(this).attr("value") == "" || $(this).attr("value") == $(this).attr('placeholder')){
                                        $(this).removeClass("not_empty");
                                    }else{
                                        $(this).addClass("not_empty");
                                    }
                                });

                                $(".fancy-input").focus(function(){
                                    if($(this).attr("value") == $(this).attr('placeholder')){
                                        $(this).attr("value", "");
                                    }
                                });

                                    if($(this).attr("value") == ""){

                                    }
                                });

      <div class="main_page_content">
       <div class="blogpost">
        <h1 class="title">
         <a class="blue" href="/blog/2015/05/11/how-get-best-deal-private-jet/">
          How to get the best deal on a Private Jet
         </a>
        </h1>
        <div class="pubdate">
         <div class="date">
          11 May 2015
         </div>
         Categories:
         <a href="/blog/categories/air-travel/">
          Air Travel
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="/blog/categories/infographic/">
          Infographic
         </a>
         Tags:
         <a href="/blog/tags/Airport%20Lounge/" rel="tag" title="Show all entries tagged by Airport Lounge">
          Airport Lounge
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="/blog/tags/Airports/" rel="tag" title="Show all entries tagged by Airports">
          Airports
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="/blog/tags/Business%20Travel/" rel="tag" title="Show all entries tagged by Business Travel">
          Business Travel
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="/blog/tags/Flying/" rel="tag" title="Show all entries tagged by Flying">
          Flying
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="/blog/tags/Private%20Jet/" rel="tag" title="Show all entries tagged by Private Jet">
          Private Jet
         </a>
        </div>
        <div class="content">
         <p>
          It is not much fun flying these days what with having to get to the airport two hours before your flight actually takes off and then waiting in a long queue at security as the people in front of you forget to take their laptops out of their bags in the Fast Track lane and their shoes set off the alarm and so they have to do it all again and get a pat down whilst you are waiting patiently shoes in hand, belt off ready to go.
         </p>
         <p>
          Then once you have finally got through in one piece and got dressed again there is that sense of relief and achievement.  The next challenge is then to battle your way past all those Duty Free shops and find a quiet seat in which to gather your breath before your flight is called.  Those of you lucky enough to be flying business class or have access to a lounge can immerse yourself in comfort and tranquillity whilst you wait and grab a coffee or something a little stronger depending on just how stressed you feel at that point!
         </p>
         <p>
          Once you finally make it on board the scrum begins for overhead bin space as more and more is brought into the cabin these day to avoid those hated charges the airlines levy for putting your luggage in the hold.  You then have to squeeze in between strangers who may or may not be good company for the next few hours.
         </p>
         <p>
          Although flying Business Class is marginally better, you still have to go through security and board the plane with everyone else.  The good news though is that there is now a cost-effective way to avoid all this and that is to fly on a private jet.
         </p>
         <p>
          I can hear you already saying there is no way can I afford to fly on a private jet.  Well you may well be surprised to learn that you can sometimes fly on an empty leg flight for as little as 145 per person or even as little as 800 to 2,000 for an entire jet!  This generally means no baggage restrictions, hassle-free security, not having to get to the airport two hours early and you are less likely to suffer delays due to bad weather or other problems commercial airlines tend to suffer from.
         </p>
         <p>
          The infographic below put together by
          <a href="https://www.buddyloans.com/blog/how-to-get-a-deal-on-a-private-jet/">
           Buddy Loans
          </a>
          takes you through a few tips on just how easy it is to get a good deal on a private jet.
         </p>
         <p>
          <img alt="Private Jet Infographic" class="None" src="/media/cache/photos/how-to-get-a-deal-on-a-private-jet_jpg_660x4500_crop_upscale_q90.jpg"/>
         </p>
         <div class="clear">
         </div>
        </div>

            function CheckForm13(f) {
                var email_re = /[a-z0-9!#$%&amp;'*+\/=?^_`{|}~-]+(?:\.[a-z0-9!#$%&amp;'*+\/=?^_`{|}~-]+)*@(?:[a-z0-9](?:[a-z0-9-]*[a-z0-9])?\.)+[a-z0-9](?:[a-z0-9-]*[a-z0-9])?/i;
                if (!email_re.test(f.email.value)) {
                    alert("Please enter your email address.");
                    f.email.focus();
                    return false;
                }

                $("#newsletter-form-holder").addClass('loading');
                $("#newsletter-form").fadeTo('fast', 0.2);

                setTimeout(function(){
                    $("#newsletter-form-holder").load('/user/a_subscribe_to_newsletter/',
                            { email: f.email.value},

                                $("#newsletter-form-holder").removeClass('loading');

  <script type="text/javascript">
   $(document).ready(function(){
            // classes for convenient IE styling
            $("li:last", "ul").addClass("last");
            $("li:first", "ul").addClass("first");
            $("a.fancybox").fancybox();

            // the "i" tooltips in forms:
            // FIXME: should't we use jquery.tools for tooltips?
            $('.form li[title]').each(function(){
                $(this).append('&lt;div class="tooltip"&gt;&lt;div class="content"&gt;'+$(this).attr('title')+'&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;');
                $(this).attr('title', '').addClass('has_tooltip').find('label:eq(0)').addClass('i');

            });
            $('.form li.has_tooltip').mouseenter(function(){
                if(!$(this).hasClass('animation')){
                    $(this).find('.tooltip').fadeIn(function(){
                        $(this).parent('li').removeClass('animation');
                    });
                }
            });
            $('.form li.has_tooltip').mouseleave(function(){
                $(this).addClass('animation');
                $(this).find('.tooltip').fadeOut(300, function(){
                    $(this).parent('li').removeClass('animation');
                });
            });
        });
  </script>

                errorClass: "form_error",
                errorPlacement: function(error, element) {
                    error.appendTo(element.parents('li'));
                }
            });
        });
